killing in jerusalem and billy straight featuring hollywood homicide detective petra connor his new novel flesh and blood will be published in hardcover in fall he is also the author of numerous essays short stories and scientific articles two childrens books and three volumes of psychology including savage spawn reflections on violent children he and his wife the novelist faye kellerman have four children
